benefit the economic development of india scholarship in teaching and learning scholarship in research and creative accomplishments and relevance to industry are three driving forces for us at iit jodhpur iit jodhpur functions from its sprawling residential permanent campus of acres on national highway north northwest of jodhpur towards nagaur this campus is meticulously planned and envisioned welcome to the engineering science message from chairperson es undergratuate commitee engineering applications generally require multidisciplinary knowledge spanning across various disciplines of engineering and sciences knowledge in humanities along with engineering and or sciences are also finding important applications tech in engineering sciences es is unique bachelors degree program of iit jodhpur which aim to impart core knowledge in two targeted focus areas in science and engineering to meet demands of emerging industrial and academic requirements any student admitted to iit jodhpur can opt for tech in engineering science post st year students will be required to complete core courses of es in the first two years of study whereas they can outline their own curriculum in the guidance of faculty advisor in the form of electives for the remaining two years from courses across disciplines of engineering science and humanities in line with regular tech programs students can also use credits out of stipulated electives and additional credits to earn minor specialization as an add on to the tech degree the flexibility of curriculum selection as per students capabilities and interest with faculty guidance aims to impartsufficient knowledge to the students to be future ready professionals institute background and vision innovations scientific discoveries and new technologies are the essential foundations of the indian institute of technology jodhpur the institute focuseson building solid and in depth knowledge in the engineering domains and strongly encourages interdisciplinary learning the courses offered are defined such that it enhances the imagination and creativity of the students to identify and solve new problems in society our endeavour is to build an atmosphere for uninhibited ideas the institute offers tech programs computer science engineering electrical engineering engineering sciences artificial intelligence and data science mechanical engineering bioengineering materials engineering chemical engineering and civil and infrastructure engineering the institute also empowers students by allowing them to avail specializations minors and elective courses program background engineering science is unique branch of engineering designed to cater to the upcoming demand of the industry and research training the best of students to have strong foundation in every field along with specialization in their topic of interest our institute is one of the primary institutes offering an engineering science program this programme is four year course the first two years are devoted to topics which we believe all engineering undergraduates should study in the third and fourth years the students have the opportunity to study any two complementary disciplines by drafting their own course structure this fosters multi disciplinary thinking and integrated application of engineering scientific and mathematical principles in young students the students can specialise minor in any field as well redirecttologinpage

message from chairperson es undergratuate commitee engineering applications generally require multidisciplinary knowledge spanning across various disciplines of engineering and sciences knowledge in humanities along with engineering and or sciences are also finding important applications tech in engineering sciences es is unique bachelors degree program of iit jodhpur which aim to impart core knowledge in two targeted focus areas in science and engineering to meet demands of emerging industrial and academic requirements any student admitted to iit jodhpur can opt for tech in engineering science post st year students will be required to complete core courses of es in the first two years of study whereas they can outline their own curriculum in the guidance of faculty advisor in the form of electives for the remaining two years from courses across disciplines of engineering science and humanities in line with regular tech programs students can also use credits out of stipulated electives and additional credits to earn minor specialization as an add on to the tech degree the flexibility of curriculum selection as per students capabilities and interest with faculty guidance aims to impartsufficient knowledge to the students to be future ready professionals
message from chairperson es undergratuate commitee
engineering applications generally require multidisciplinary knowledge spanning across various disciplines of engineering and sciences knowledge in humanities along with engineering and or sciences are also finding important applications tech in engineering sciences es is unique bachelors degree program of iit jodhpur which aim to impart core knowledge in two targeted focus areas in science and engineering to meet demands of emerging industrial and academic requirements
any student admitted to iit jodhpur can opt for tech in engineering science post st year students will be required to complete core courses of es in the first two years of study whereas they can outline their own curriculum in the guidance of faculty advisor in the form of electives for the remaining two years from courses across disciplines of engineering science and humanities in line with regular tech programs students can also use credits out of stipulated electives and additional credits to earn minor specialization as an add on to the tech degree the flexibility of curriculum selection as per students capabilities and interest with faculty guidance aims to impartsufficient knowledge to the students to be future ready professionals
institute background and vision innovations scientific discoveries and new technologies are the essential foundations of the indian institute of technology jodhpur the institute focuseson building solid and in depth knowledge in the engineering domains and strongly encourages interdisciplinary learning the courses offered are defined such that it enhances the imagination and creativity of the students to identify and solve new problems in society our endeavour is to build an atmosphere for uninhibited ideas the institute offers tech programs computer science engineering electrical engineering engineering sciences artificial intelligence and data science mechanical engineering bioengineering materials engineering chemical engineering and civil and infrastructure engineering the institute also empowers students by allowing them to avail specializations minors and elective courses
institute background and vision
innovations scientific discoveries and new technologies are the essential foundations of the indian institute of technology jodhpur the institute focuseson building solid and in depth knowledge in the engineering domains and strongly encourages interdisciplinary learning the courses offered are defined such that it enhances the imagination and creativity of the students to identify and solve new problems in society our endeavour is to build an atmosphere for uninhibited ideas the institute offers tech programs computer science engineering electrical engineering engineering sciences artificial intelligence and data science mechanical engineering bioengineering materials engineering chemical engineering and civil and infrastructure engineering the institute also empowers students by allowing them to avail specializations minors and elective courses
program background engineering science is unique branch of engineering designed to cater to the upcoming demand of the industry and research training the best of students to have strong foundation in every field along with specialization in their topic of interest our institute is one of the primary institutes offering an engineering science program this programme is four year course the first two years are devoted to topics which we believe all engineering undergraduates should study in the third and fourth years the students have the opportunity to study any two complementary disciplines by drafting their own course structure this fosters multi disciplinary thinking and integrated application of engineering scientific and mathematical principles in young students the students can specialise minor in any field as well
engineering science is unique branch of engineering designed to cater to the upcoming demand of the industry and research training the best of students to have strong foundation in every field along with specialization in their topic of interest our institute is one of the primary institutes offering an engineering science program this programme is four year course the first two years are devoted to topics which we believe all engineering undergraduates should study in the third and fourth years the students have the opportunity to study any two complementary disciplines by drafting their own course structure this fosters multi disciplinary thinking and integrated application of engineering scientific and mathematical principles in young students the students can specialise minor in any field as well

welcome to the office of research development the office of provides specialized administrative and managerial support for the operation of sponsored research projects consultancy projects and other related activities of the institute the office of facilitates interaction with national and international agencies supporting research development also it promotes academia industry interactions and collaboration with larger laboratories and liaises between institute and funding agencies further it supports faculty members in filing of patents and documenting ipr generated through research activity of the institute the office of facilitates the following management of projects registration of sponsored consulting and institute projects raising invoice grants in aid bill receiving funds prepare utilization certificates appointment extension and resignations of project staff members payment of salary work related to fellowships project related purchases imports and their payments management of temporary advances to pis and project staff members settlement of advances payment for work assignments and preparation of cheques bank reconciliation accounts preparation management of investments management of office preparation and publishing of booklets hard and soft copies related to office of newsletter institute research magazine developing maintaining database of contacts in industry academia and organisations in india and abroad designing and preparing flyers of different departments and laboratories of the institute and managing mous iprs corporate communications events and relationships latest news live updates applications for international mobility research grant imrg are invited from the new faculty members who are yet to complete years from the date of joining form no and travel within india from project fund as per the office order no iitj reg dated th july it is mandatory to obtain prior approval from the dean of research and development dord through the the office of provides specialized administrative and managerial support for the operation of sponsored research projects consultancy projects and other related activities of the institute the office of facilitates interaction with national and international agencies supporting research development also it promotes academia industry interactions and collaboration with larger laboratories and liaises between institute and funding agencies further it supports faculty members in filing of patents and documenting ipr generated through research activity of the institute the office of facilitates the following
management of projects registration of sponsored consulting and institute projects raising invoice grants in aid bill receiving funds prepare utilization certificates appointment extension and resignations of project staff members payment of salary work related to fellowships project related purchases imports and their payments management of temporary advances to pis and project staff members settlement of advances payment for work assignments and preparation of cheques bank reconciliation accounts preparation management of investments management of office preparation and publishing of booklets hard and soft copies related to office of newsletter institute research magazine developing maintaining database of contacts in industry academia and organisations in india and abroad designing and preparing flyers of different departments and laboratories of the institute and managing mous iprs corporate communications events and relationships

welcome to the department of computer science engineering computer science and engineering today plays major role in transforming every aspect of human life in addressing social challenges and catalyzing the ongoing wave of the industrial revolution the department is driven by its commitment to excel in next generation technology development and research our mission is to strengthen industry academia collaborations and prepare our students to contribute to multi disciplinary projects and for solving problems of national interest vision to be among the top departments in terms of research contributions practical impact and applications of computer science and engineering in the country in the next years and internationally well known in some focused areas in the next years some of our missions are to achieve excellence in research in fundamental as well as applied areas of cse and allied subject for innovative discoveries develop an academic ecosystem by collaborating and develop and support the notion of computing for all across disciplines at the institute mission our missions are to achieve excellence in research in fundamental as well as applied areas of cse and allied subject for innovative discoveries develop an academic ecosystem by collaborating and develop and support the notion of computing for all across disciplines at the institute achieving excellence in research in fundamental as well as applied areas of cse and allied subjects for innovative discoveries develop an academic ecosystem by collaborating within the institute as well by means of international national and regional institutes the collaborations may be fostered by research visits collaborative projects joint thesis internship guidance research mentoring etc develop and support the notion of computing for all across disciplines at the institute embracing shared dialogue across disciplines and encouraging experiential learning to redefine the contours of traditional computer science teaching and learning be one of the leading departments in the country for hybrid cse education define and solve real world problems in collaboration with industry and develop industry connect by means of research grants consultancies and collaborative projects develop start up ecosystem in emerging areas of computing in collaboration with other departments at iit jodhpur welcome to the department of computer science engineering
welcome to the department of computer science engineering
computer science and engineering today plays major role in transforming every aspect of human life in addressing social challenges and catalyzing the ongoing wave of the industrial revolution the department is driven by its commitment to excel in next generation technology development and research our mission is to strengthen industry academia collaborations and prepare our students to contribute to multi disciplinary projects and for solving problems of national interest
computer science and engineering today plays major role in transforming every aspect of human life in addressing social challenges and catalyzing the ongoing wave of the industrial revolution the department is driven by its commitment to excel in next generation technology development and research our mission is to strengthen industry academia collaborations and prepare our students to contribute to multi disciplinary projects and for solving problems of national interest
vision to be among the top departments in terms of research contributions practical impact and applications of computer science and engineering in the country in the next years and internationally well known in some focused areas in the next years some of our missions are to achieve excellence in research in fundamental as well as applied areas of cse and allied subject for innovative discoveries develop an academic ecosystem by collaborating and develop and support the notion of computing for all across disciplines at the institute mission our missions are to achieve excellence in research in fundamental as well as applied areas of cse and allied subject for innovative discoveries develop an academic ecosystem by collaborating and develop and support the notion of computing for all across disciplines at the institute achieving excellence in research in fundamental as well as applied areas of cse and allied subjects for innovative discoveries develop an academic ecosystem by collaborating within the institute as well by means of international national and regional institutes the collaborations may be fostered by research visits collaborative projects joint thesis internship guidance research mentoring etc develop and support the notion of computing for all across disciplines at the institute embracing shared dialogue across disciplines and encouraging experiential learning to redefine the contours of traditional computer science teaching and learning be one of the leading departments in the country for hybrid cse education define and solve real world problems in collaboration with industry and develop industry connect by means of research grants consultancies and collaborative projects develop start up ecosystem in emerging areas of computing in collaboration with other departments at iit jodhpur dissemination of knowledge without physical boundaries classroom online and other modes of teaching to create workforce which is ready to ethically solve technological challenges of the next generation provide thought leadership in public policy and ethics of emerging computing technologies towards building an equitable and ethical society

welcome to the department of electrical engineering the department of electrical engineering primarily focuses on imparting quality education and preparing students to face future technological challenges the vision of the department is to enhance the research environment and to innovate in pedagogy to address the challenges of socio economic and human resource development the department is committed to engage in high quality research by faculty members and students and in the pursuit of excellence in teaching the department offers tech in electrical engineering with broad range of major and minor specializations and three state of the art tech programs in sensors and internet of things siot cyber physical systems cps and intelligent communication systems ics the department also runs dual degree tech ph programs in intelligent communication systems sensors and internet of things siot and cyber physical systems cps as well as ph program with broad range of specializations covering detailed aspects of microelectronics signal processing communication microwave photonics power systems control systems etc the department is also starting new executive mtech program in intelligent vlsi systems for working professionals from july the prospective undergraduate and postgraduate students are encouraged to visit the academic programs ug program pg programs and doctoral programs page of the department to know more about the details of courses offered in the department to know more about the current research themes of the faculty members the prospective students are encouraged to visit the research overview page of the department technology tracks currently pursued by the department include emerging and challenging fields that culminate at the intersection of several traditional research areas current technology tracks active collaboration is on going with organizations like freescale semiconductors global foundries aiims jodhpur dst drdo and isro to name few the department has been attracting various sponsored projects from organizations since its inception consolidated year wise cutoffs of last four years download file kb highlights view all highlights dr saakshi dhanekar associate professor in department of electrical engineering iit jodhpur published manuscript in the chemical engineering journal impact factor ph student mr prabhanshu yadav won the best paper award in ieee international conference on advanced networks and telecommunications systems dr akshay moudgil awarded teaching excellence award latest news view all news result of ph welcome to the department of electrical engineering
the department of electrical engineering primarily focuses on imparting quality education and preparing students to face future technological challenges the vision of the department is to enhance the research environment and to innovate in pedagogy to address the challenges of socio economic and human resource development the department is committed to engage in high quality research by faculty members and students and in the pursuit of excellence in teaching the department offers tech in electrical engineering with broad range of major and minor specializations and three state of the art tech programs in sensors and internet of things siot cyber physical systems cps and intelligent communication systems ics the department also runs dual degree tech ph programs in intelligent communication systems sensors and internet of things siot and cyber physical systems cps as well as ph program with broad range of specializations covering detailed aspects of microelectronics signal processing communication microwave photonics power systems control systems etc the department is also starting new executive mtech program in intelligent vlsi systems for working professionals from july the prospective undergraduate and postgraduate students are encouraged to visit the academic programs ug program pg programs and doctoral programs page of the department to know more about the details of courses offered in the department to know more about the current research themes of the faculty members the prospective students are encouraged to visit the research overview page of the department technology tracks currently pursued by the department include emerging and challenging fields that culminate at the intersection of several traditional research areas

welcome to the office of students the office of students acts as link between students student facilities faculty and the administration of iit jodhpur the sole motive of the office is to create an atmosphere that promotes personal and academic development of students by organizing various activities and programs and providing them necessary support thereby enhancing the overall student experience during their tenure at iit jodhpur the office is headed by the associate dean students and its activities are coordinated by assistant registrar students superintendent students project staff and officers scope since its inception the office of students has been working extensively towards integration of activities by streamlining various processes the core purviews of the office of students may be categorized under the following administration the office corresponds with the ministries government agencies regarding various scholarships workshops events conferences etc disbursal of teaching assistantship conducting orientation program for new students issuance of various certificates namely bonafide certificate no objection certificate character certificate etc academics the office has launched two non graded credit courses on social connect responsibility and performing arts from the academic year the aim of launching these courses is to help the incoming students to connect socially and explore their potential that will in turn shape their overall personality student activities student activities that form major domain under the office range from but are not limited to gymkhana activities counseling services alumni relations and placements and internships outreach programs various outreach programs are organized by the office with the aim of creating awareness about various government private schemes that can be beneficial to the students few recent outreach programs to mention are the cii workshop on prime minister fellowship for doctoral research and the visit discussion with mr naval jit kapoor joint secretary ministry of tribal affairs regarding scholarship schemes and grievance redressal responsibilities the responsibilities of office of students include the following disbursement of teaching assistantship providing guidance for students regarding various state and national level scholarships fee remissions for sc st ews students effectuating various workshops non graded courses etc coordinating and supervising student gymkhana activities under different societies enthusing students to conduct and participate in cultural events rendering support to students in organizing various festivals like ignus varchas nimble spandan and various other cultural literary events like spicmacay programs facilitating and overseeing student election process and working with the elected students representatives on various issues concerning the students during their period of stay at iit jodhpur managing student hostels and mess dining facilities and other amenities within the campus guiding and preparing students for internships placements organizing training programs to make the students employable and equip them with the skills essential to build rewarding career for themselves constantly working towards student wellbeing through counseling services and helping them to achieve higher levels of maturity and motivation key functionaries ankita sharma dean of students affairs dosa redirecttologinpage
welcome to the office of students
welcome to the office of students
the office of students acts as link between students student facilities faculty and the administration of iit jodhpur the sole motive of the office is to create an atmosphere that promotes personal and academic development of students by organizing various activities and programs and providing them necessary support thereby enhancing the overall student experience during their tenure at iit jodhpur the office is headed by the associate dean students and its activities are coordinated by assistant registrar students superintendent students project staff and officers
the office of students acts as link between students student facilities faculty and the administration of iit jodhpur the sole motive of the office is to create an atmosphere that promotes personal and academic development of students by organizing various activities and programs and providing them necessary support thereby enhancing the overall student experience during their tenure at iit jodhpur the office is headed by the associate dean students and its activities are coordinated by assistant registrar students superintendent students project staff and officers
scope since its inception the office of students has been working extensively towards integration of activities by streamlining various processes the core purviews of the office of students may be categorized under the following administration the office corresponds with the ministries government agencies regarding various scholarships workshops events conferences etc disbursal of teaching assistantship conducting orientation program for new students issuance of various certificates namely bonafide certificate no objection certificate character certificate etc academics the office has launched two non graded credit courses on social connect responsibility and performing arts from the academic year the aim of launching these courses is to help the incoming students to connect socially and explore their potential that will in turn shape their overall personality student activities student activities that form major domain under the office range from but are not limited to gymkhana activities counseling services alumni relations and placements and internships outreach programs various outreach programs are organized by the office with the aim of creating awareness about various government private schemes that can be beneficial to the students few recent outreach programs to mention are the cii workshop on prime minister fellowship for doctoral research and the visit discussion with mr naval jit kapoor joint secretary ministry of tribal affairs regarding scholarship schemes and grievance redressal
since its inception the office of students has been working extensively towards integration of activities by streamlining various processes the core purviews of the office of students may be categorized under the following
administration the office corresponds with the ministries government agencies regarding various scholarships workshops events conferences etc disbursal of teaching assistantship conducting orientation program for new students issuance of various certificates namely bonafide certificate no objection certificate character certificate etc
academics the office has launched two non graded credit courses on social connect responsibility and performing arts from the academic year the aim of launching these courses is to help the incoming students to connect socially and explore their potential that will in turn shape their overall personality
student activities student activities that form major domain under the office range from but are not limited to gymkhana activities counseling services alumni relations and placements and internships
outreach programs various outreach programs are organized by the office with the aim of creating awareness about various government private schemes that can be beneficial to the students few recent outreach programs to mention are the cii workshop on prime minister fellowship for doctoral research and the visit discussion with mr naval jit kapoor joint secretary ministry of tribal affairs regarding scholarship schemes and grievance redressal
responsibilities the responsibilities of office of students include the following disbursement of teaching assistantship providing guidance for students regarding various state and national level scholarships fee remissions for sc st ews students effectuating various workshops non graded courses etc coordinating and supervising student gymkhana activities under different societies enthusing students to conduct and participate in cultural events rendering support to students in organizing various festivals like ignus varchas nimble spandan and various other cultural literary events like spicmacay programs facilitating and overseeing student election process and working with the elected students representatives on various issues concerning the students during their period of stay at iit jodhpur managing student hostels and mess dining facilities and other amenities within the campus guiding and preparing students for internships placements organizing training programs to make the students employable and equip them with the skills essential to build rewarding career for themselves constantly working towards student wellbeing through counseling services and helping them to achieve higher levels of maturity and motivation
the responsibilities of office of students include the following
disbursement of teaching assistantship providing guidance for students regarding various state and national level scholarships fee remissions for sc st ews students
effectuating various workshops non graded courses etc
coordinating and supervising student gymkhana activities under different societies
enthusing students to conduct and participate in cultural events rendering support to students in organizing various festivals like ignus varchas nimble spandan and various other cultural literary events like spicmacay programs
facilitating and overseeing student election process and working with the elected students representatives on various issues concerning the students during their period of stay at iit jodhpur
managing student hostels and mess dining facilities and other amenities within the campus
guiding and preparing students for internships placements organizing training programs to make the students employable and equip them with the skills essential to build rewarding career for themselves
constantly working towards student wellbeing through counseling services and helping them to achieve higher levels of maturity and motivation

welcome to the office of executive education transformative odyssey for visionary trailblazers pioneering learning frontiers dynamic forward thinking programs meticulously crafted to empower professionals with the acumen and foresight to spearhead innovation helmed by iit jodhpur esteemed faculty and industry luminaries our courses seamlessly weave groundbreaking research with practical applications honing critical thinking and strategic mastery comprehensive empowerment tailored for ambitious professionals our executive education offerings present an adaptable learning ecosystem spanning in person online and hybrid modalities participants thrive in an intellectually stimulating milieu fortified by seamless administrative facilitation and unparalleled access to cutting edge resources ensuring profoundly enriching and frictionless educational voyage enduring alliances transcending conventional academia our programs foster deep rooted professional synergies enrolees become part of an illustrious nexus of industry stalwarts visionaries and policymakers paving the way for transformative collaborations and unparalleled career avenues purposeful heterogeneity we convene confluence of professionals hailing from myriad sectors regions and disciplines catalysing rich tapestry of intellectual exchange this cultivated diversity fortifies leadership prowess augments cross sector problem solving and equips participants to adeptly navigate the labyrinth of contemporary global challenges vision to make iit jodhpur leading indian institute offering world class executive education for working professionals and other aspirants mission to provide well curated programmes in line with industry requirements provide opportunity to learners via both offline and online modes develop partnership with online edu service providers the best in the business draw industry attention to iitj academic activities provide up to date insights and knowledge to participants gain access to ongoing and upcoming industry practices industry connect and participate in industry meet generate revenue streams executive programmes structure at glance executive tech programs credits credit contact hours executive postgraduate diploma credits executive postgraduate certificate credits executive mba programs credits executive undergraduate programs year certification credits year diploma welcome to the digital infrastructure automation computer center the digital infrastructure automation dia commonly known as computer center of the indian institute of technology jodhpur stands as testament to the institution commitment to cutting edge research innovation and technological development as pivotal hub for computing and information technology the computer center has played crucial role in shaping the academic landscape and the advancement of the institute since its inception the computer center has undergone remarkable development and growth aligning itself with advancements in the field of computing equipped with state of the art infrastructure and team of highly skilled professionals the center has fostered an environment conducive to research and learning read more quick access erp portal private cloud moodle lab booking system dia verticals computer center network cybersecurity erp automation objective the center primary objective is to provide computational resources technical support and expertise to students faculty members and researchers across various disciplines its advanced computing facilities include high performance computing clusters ai supercomputers and specialized software these resources empower the iit jodhpur community to undertake complex computational tasks simulate intricate models and conduct data intensive research learn more redirecttologinpage

academic regulations back to index introduction back to index academic programmes at indian institute of technology jodhpur are designed to develop thehighest calibre human resource capable of understanding the new patterns of knowledgecreation across disciplines obliterating traditional boundaries between science humanities social sciences and engineering iit jodhpur aims to produce quality professionals who would beable to address profound and wide ranging societal challenges of the st century such asenergy food water housing mobility and health in addition to imparting scientificknowledge iit jodhpur endeavours to inculcate human qualities of courage integrity fairness humility and team effort among its graduates through curricular co curricular andextra curricular activities on campus the undergraduate academic programmes focus on developing temper for the life longprocess of learning creative thinking and exploring the postgraduate academic programmesfocus on developing deep understanding of the subject of study coupled with creativeinquisitiveness and the ability to address and solve new problems with free and objectivemind the academic programmes are based on three tenets of semester system creditsystem and relative grading these academic programmes are administered by dulyconstituted academic committee ac through the office of academics the ac will be chairedby dean academics in the absence of dean academics associate dean academics pg associate dean academics ug will discharge the responsibilities of dean academics the senate of the institute has formulated set of guidelines and rules to ensure highstandard of performance as well as for smooth functioning of the academic programmes withinthis broad set of guidelines subject to the approval of senate different programmes caninclude additional academic requirements as deemed necessary for that programme theseacademic programmes are continuously monitored by the senate and make appropriatemodifications improvements as and when necessary academic session back to index the academic session normally runs from the end of july in one year to the middle of july in the next year the academic session is divided into three parts two regular semesters and summer term as per the following timelines semester from the fourth week of july to the last week of november semester ii from the last week of december to the last week of april summer term from the middle of may to the middle of july excluding the days of the examinations the total number of days of instruction in semester is at least academic calendar back to index the academic calendar gives the exact dates of all important events during the academic session such as orientation registration the commencement of classes adding and dropping of courses submission of documents examinations submission of grades project evaluation declaration of results mid semester recess and vacation this calendar is approved by the senate registration back to index students are required to register for prescribed credits as per the programme on the dates specified in the academic calendar if the student does not register by the date of registration she he can register by paying the fine and register before the date of late registration provisional registration fresh student joining the institute who is awaiting the final results of the qualifying examination is allowed to register provisionally on submission of certificate from her his last institute stating that she he has appeared in the final examination of the qualifying degree the student is required to submit documents of having passed the qualifying examination by the last date given in the academic calendar for the registration to be regularized late registration if the student does not register by the date of late registration as mentioned in the academic calendar he she will be deregistered the appeal against deregistration may be made to chairman senate through dean academics chairman senate may permit the continuation of registration on payment of an appropriate fine adding and dropping of courses student may add or drop course with approval ofthe faculty advisor till the last date of registration withdrawing from course after the last date of add drop student will have theoption of withdrawing from course the last date of course withdrawal will be typically withinfour weeks from the beginning of the semester as specified in the academic calendar thewithdrawn course will be mentioned in the student grade card with letter grade cancellation of semester registration absence for period of four or more weeksduring semester shall result in automatic cancellation of the registration of student from allthe courses in that semester summer course registration department may offer summer courses to enable thestudents to clear their backlog courses and or regular credit courses course will run duringsummer provided faculty member is available for running the course the course is offeredon approval of the dean teaching and evaluation back to index teaching back to index medium of instruction the medium of instruction is english all courses have associated credits credits of course is based on the number of contact hours for lectures tutorials and practicals student on successful completion of the course with passing grade will earn equivalent number of credits based on required academic maturity level of students for attending course course is assigned level course can consist of independent components which can be completed independently these components are called fractals course is identified by unique number following tables define all parameters related to course numbering scheme table course code description course code descriptions offering department idrp course type level of courses unique identification number indicates fractal categories see table see table see table this code will be given centrally by the office of academics regular fractal fractal fractal note examples of course codes course title course code regular course engineering mechanics mel xx fractal course robotics types of courses course type category lecture courses other than lecture hours these courses can have tutorial and practical hours structures etc practical practice based courses where performance is evaluated primarily on the basis of practice practical or laboratory work with ltp structures such as etc project based courses major minor mini projects non graded core component thesis seminar courses independent study product realization engineering design graded and non graded table level of courses category and credit requirements level category credit requirements courses for tech programmes tech cr tech cr tech cr preparatory courses of sc and tech programmes not open to tech and tech tech dual degree tech cr sc cr courses for sc programmes tech cr sc cr tech cr courses for tech programmes tech cr sc cr tech cr ph cr advanced courses for sc advanced courses for tech and ph programmes an level course should have level course as pre requisite tech cr ph cr approval of courses the senate approves each course along with its weight in terms of credits only the approved courses may be offered during any semester summer term list of courses the list of courses to be offered in program is finalized before the beginning of the semester by the department hosting that program categories of courses courses offered can be from one of the following categories regular course regular course has hours of class room engagement per one credit regular course can be under elective or core compulsory categories elective courses of or level will run if minimum of students register for the course or level elective course can run with minimum of registered students course not running as regular course may be offered as self study course as per the following section self study course self study course will be from the list of courses approved by senate the main features of self study course are as follows student may be allowed to register for an elective course as self study course provided that the course is not running in that semester as regular course or student is not on campus during the course with prior approval of the competent authority student may also be permitted to register for core or program compulsory course in self study mode provided he she has failed in it earlier and the course is not being offered as regular course during that semester or student is not on campus during the course with prior approval of the competent authority students should apply for self study course with the appropriate recommendation of course coordinator and dugc drc interdisciplinary program committee the final sanction of self study course to student is made by the dean academics formal classroom engagement may not be there for self study course but laboratory design and computation exercises will be conducted if they form an integral part of the course the course coordinator conducts the assessment as per the evaluation norms for the award of letter grade at the end of the semester self study course will appear with the approved course title on the transcript independent study course independent study enables student to pursue course credit on an academic topic of interestunder the supervision of faculty member the term independent does not mean not involvingan instructor but independent of regular class engagement self disciplined and having senseof own direction and goals are fundamental requirements of an independent study course astudent having cgpa more than or equal to can opt for independent study courses with therecommendation of supervising professor the main features of an independent study courseare as follows student may be permitted to register for topic of interest as an independent studycourse not exceeding credits in self study mode at most once during the program such independent study course will be counted toward open elective requirements of theprogram and will appear with the title independent study on the transcript students should apply for an independent study course with the appropriaterecommendation of course coordinator and dugc drc irc the final sanction of anindependent study course to student is made by the dean academics normally no formal lectures will be held for an independent study course butlaboratory design and computation exercises will be conducted if they form an integralpart of the course conduct of courses each course is conducted by the instructor with the assistance of the required number of tutors as needed the instructor is responsible for conducting the course evaluating the performance of students awarding the grades at the end of the semester and transmitting the grades as per subsection course approved by the senate of iit jodhpur can be conducted through either direct contact ii synchronized remote contact iii guided study mode or combination of these in direct contact mode coordinator or instructor will have face to face physical interaction with the students synchronized remote contact mode would require the faculty and or the students to be concurrently connected to the class room interaction via electronic conferencing involving both audio and video communication however there has to be direct interaction between faculty and students for limited hours typically of the stipulated contact hours in guided study mode faculty would guide single or group of students to take up study of an approved course via self learning and discussion oriented contact sessions this mode can be also adopted for enabling student to take up study of new course not yet approved by the senate under supervision of faculty all formal evaluation component applicable to courses being run through any one of the above mentioned modes will be conducted under direct physical supervision of faculty all laboratory component of course requiring use of specialized facility will be conducted through direct contact the student shall have access to his her answer paper of all the written examinations conducted for given course which may be shown to him her by the instructor concerned the instructor must keep all evaluation records in his custody at least for the next six months teaching assignments the instructors and tutors for all courses to be offered during the semester are allocated by the head of the department hosting the program when faculty members of other departments are also required to participate in teaching particular course the allocation shall be done in consultation with the head of that department auditing of courses student may audit course in addition to the prescribed academic load requirement with the permission of the instructor of the course being audited and the faculty advisor under this arrangement the course will be listed in the grade card of the student attendance requirements student should have full attendance in each course unless the student takes leave of absence for valid reasons the student has to attend every lecture tutorial or lab session the attendance records must be made available to the student after every lecture even if the student attendance falls below the student will be allowed to appear for the exams students not meeting the attendance criterion of will be required to score at least grade to pass course these students would be awarded grade if their marks are lower than the cut off for grade in course evaluation back to index the performance of students in course is evaluated continuously using their interaction in the classroom and performances in examinations the laboratory work if any and term papers and projects the performance of students in course is evaluated through examinations and on continuous basis the senate will decide from time to time on the system of tests and examinations in each subject in each semester minor minor and major examinations are mandatory components of the evaluation of regular week long lecture course the minor examinations shall be of minutes duration and the major examination of minutes fractal courses less than credits must have at least one examination the total weightage of examination component three examinations for week long course shall be between to of the total weightage of evaluation measure evaluation policy has to be known from the first day of the class the continuous evaluation may include but not limited to interaction in the classroom quizzes assignments tutorials laboratory work term papers and projects grading system back to index letter grades back to index letter grades at the end of the semester student is awarded relative letter grade in each course by the instructor offering the course considering the performance of the student during the semester with respect to those of the other students registered in the course it is proposed that ten regular letter grades namely and shall be awarded in each course each letter grade is associated with numerical equivalent on point scale shown in table in addition there are four special letter grades namely and which stand for incomplete satisfactory thesis continuation and unsatisfactory respectively the faculty member shall upload grade on the portal as per the stipulated time schedule table letter grade and its equivalent grade points letter grade grade points comment exceptional outstanding excellent very good good average below average marginal poor fail incomplete satisfactory in course thesis continuation unsatisfactory withdrawn detailed description of some of the grades is given below grades description grade has the same grade point as grade the grade indicates exceptional performance and is awarded only in the course in which the number of registered students is more than it should not exceed of the total strength of the particular theory or lab course the grade is not awarded for projects seminars grade will be awarded to student who has scored marks less than the cutoff marks for grade and has met the attendance criterion of the institute students who obtain an grade will be eligible to appear in an additional examination if they perform satisfactorily they become eligible for getting the grade converted to grade otherwise they will continue to have grade the student will have only one chance to appear for the additional examination for an grade the additional examination will be conducted within the first week of the next semester the date of additional examination of institute core courses for undergraduate students centrally notified while for all other courses the date would be announced by the respective course coordinators student can appear for maximum of three such additional tests in given semester if student cannot appear for the test due to any reason he she will not get any additional chance if student with grade in course does not pass the course through the additional test or obtains an grade in the course he she has to repeat the course if it is core course in case the course is an elective the student may take the same course again or any other course and grades are not counted in the calculation of the cgpa however these are taken into account in the calculation of the sgpa an grade is temporarily awarded to student on his her request to denote incomplete performance in course on approval of instructor an grade is awarded in case missing an evaluation component due to absence on medical grounds or other special circumstances requests for grade should be made at the earliest but not later than the last day of major tests all evaluation requirements for such students in the corresponding course should be completed before the end of the first week of the next semester upon completion of all course requirements the grade is converted to regular grade this grade is awarded to student with satisfactory performance in non graded and audit courses if the stipulated requirements are not fulfilled the unsatisfactory grade is awarded the grades obtained in an audit course are not considered in the calculation of sgpa or cgpa this grade is awarded to student with satisfactory performance in thesis for continuation this grade is awarded to student with unsatisfactory performance in thesis audit or non graded courses this grade is awarded to student who has opted to withdraw from course withdrawal from course is permitted until the date specified in the academics calendar procedure for declaration of results back to index the following procedure would be followed for declaration of results and time line would be as per academic calendar evaluation scheme to be displayed by instructors at the start of semester display of answer sheets and all scores by instructors finalization of grades by instructorsgrade moderation by department institute level committee for department institute wide coursesrecommendation of grades by the head of the department after scrutiny of grades by moderation committeedisplay of grades by instructorsgrade correction if any within hours of display of grades after approval of the head of the departmentapproval of grade by the dean ug pg associate dean ug pgs finalization of results by the dean ug pg associate dean ug pg approval of results by the chairman senateresults once approved cannot be changed under any circumstance in exceptional cases the student may appeal to the chairman senate for reconsideration with formal justification grade point averages back to index semester grade point average the semester grade point average sgpa is weighted average of the grades earned by student in all the courses credited by her him and reflects her his academic performance in the respective semester if the grade points associated with the letter grades earned by student in courses registered during semester are gn and the corresponding credits cn then the sgpa is given by the following formula the sgpa is calculated on the basis of grades obtained in all courses except audit courses and courses in which grade is awarded registered in particular semester cumulative grade point average the cumulative grade point average cgpa indicates the overall academic performance of student in all the courses registered up to the latest completed semester the cgpa is computed similarly as the sgpa considering all the courses in all semesters the cgpa is calculated on the basis of all pass grades except audit courses and courses in which grade is awarded obtained in all completed semesters the sgpa and cgpa calculation is based on credits earned completed at iit jodhpur alone grade card and transcript back to index grade card shall be issued to each student at the end of each semester and transcript at the end of the programme iit jodhpur grade card and transcript will only indicate the courses credits and grades completed at iit jodhpur and the total number of credits without grades earned in other academic institutions in particular semester if applicable waiver of requirements in special cases back to index the rules and regulations procedures and requirements stated in this manual other than those related to admissions to the academic programmes may be waived in special circumstances by the ac on the recommendation of the department with the approval of chairman senate all such exceptions have to be reported to the senate make up examinations back to index student who has missed minor or the major examination due to genuine reasons like illness etc may be permitted to write make up examination for the missed components the student should make an application to the dean academics through the course instructor within ten days from the date of the examination missed explaining the reasons for their absence applications received after this period need not be entertained the permission to take make up examination will be given under exceptional circumstances such as admission to hospital due to illness student needs to produce the necessary document subject to one of the following categories students residing in the hostels should produce medical certificate issued by the medical officer of the institute that he she was admitted in the hospital during the period of the missed quiz exam students residing in the hostels and taking medical consultation with outside doctors are required to obtain written permission from the medical officer of the institute hospital before they proceed for such consultation students residing in the hostels but taking medical consultation with outside doctors are required to obtain an endorsement on the certificate of treatment by the medical officer of the institute hospital student staying outside the campus permanently temporarily must produce medical certificate from the registered medical practitioner and the same should be duly endorsed by the parent guardian slot wise make up examination for major will be held during the makeup supplementary week as per academic calendar of the subsequent semester for those who are permitted to take the make up examination student who misses this make up examination will not normally be given another make up examination however in exceptional cases of prolonged illness resulting in the student missing make up examination the chairman of the senate in consultation with the dean of academics may permit the student to appear for make up examination any day before the end of the first week of the next semester under no circumstances prorating can be done for the missed examinations or attendance regulations for undergraduate programmes back to index undergraduate programs back to index iit jodhpur currently offers bachelor of technology tech programs and capability available inputs but the senate will not entertain any further appeal for review unless substantial additional information is brought to its notice leave rules back to index application for leave of assistantship during that period other leaves back to index maternity leave for ph students is sanctioned as per the directives of mhrd it will not be counted towards the maximum permissible duration of the programme any other leave may also be permissible as per the guidelines of mhrd semester withdrawal back to index may be applicable in unforeseen circumstances or for medical reasons absence for period of four or more weeks in any semester will result in automatic withdrawal from that semester in all such cases the fellowship will be stopped with immediate effect and it will be continued for only after the student rejoins the institute drc can approve and intimate office of academics regarding the leave of the student for records in case the leave extends beyond semester it can only be approved through the academic committee semester withdrawal on the medical ground will not be counted towards the maximum permissible duration of the programme for the student academic leave back to index academic leave can be requested for any of the following reasons such as fieldwork library work because of specialized collection at particular library experimental work training using specialized facility not available at iitj attending conferences workshops summer winter schools symposium collaborative work as part of joint tech ph supervision collaborative work for specific problem related to his ongoing ph programme as indicated in his research proposal exchange program as part of an exchange program with sister institution in india or abroad all such requests must be evaluated and approved by src drc irc before the leave is granted src drc irc must also make recommendations regarding continuation of fellowship during academic leave student may be allowed to spend maximum duration of one year on academic leave student during academic leave can earn maximum of credits per semester as certified by src and approved by drc financial assistance back to index applicable for non science departments the requirement of gate is exempted for an applicant with tech or equivalent post bachelor degree student may be exempted from gate as per mhrd guidelines ph student would be eligible for enhancement in the scholarship after two years provided the student has met qualifier requirement the enhanced fellowship will commence from the date of completion of both the conditions no arrears will be provided due to delay in completing the qualifier requirement the teaching research assistantship of ph student shall stop from the day of submission of the thesis rules and regulations for tech sc project back to index allotment of students to supervisors will be made based on the preferences of the students and supervisor the supervisor and area caretaker supervisor additional supervisor whenever the supervisor proceeds on short leave for period up to one year the drc irc interdisciplinary research committee shall appoint caretaker supervisor will be nominated by dean academics the chairman of irc will be member of ac one of the idrp co ordinators would be convenor of the committee the tenure for the irc will be years the irc will be approved by the dean academics change of research supervisor back to index change of supervisor under exceptional circumstances shall be permitted by dean academics on the recommendation of the drc irc after obtaining the consent of the student ii the present supervisor and iii the proposed supervisor if required realignment of student research program will happen under the supervision of the drc irc student research committee src back to index composition of src the src will normally consist of supervisor and three other faculty members conversant with the field of research with at least one member external to the department maybe outside the institute also student research committee src for the candidate shall be proposed by the supervisor recommended by the drc irc and approved by dean academics the src shall have one member identified as chairman for administrative functions and the supervisor will act as convener chairman src is to be appointed by dean academics the appointment of src should be completed by the end of the first semester any subsequent changes in the composition of src shall be communicated through the drc irc to dean academics for record chairman and supervisor shall be the internal examiners for the evaluation of the thesis the src is expected to monitor the progress of the candidate until the completion of the program annual progress monitoring meeting apm back to index the academic progress of all registered ph students will be reviewed once in year by the src and peers in the institute the review will be based upon annual progress report and ii poster presentation open to all src will award satisfactory non satisfactory grade based upon and ii two consecutive non satisfactory grades will lead to termination of registration for implementational convenience academic calendar must indicate two days in year for conducting annual progress evaluation of research scholars following the groupings of students and scheduling guidelines are suggested for students joining in st semester of ay during st july to th september of the year for students joining in nd semester of ay during st december to th february of the year the first apm will be conducted after the successful completion of qualifier requirements each semester satisfactory progress or unsatisfactory progress will be reported by the supervisor through the src for record any situation in exception to the above will be processed by the academic committee and approved by dean academics qualifier requirements of ph student back to index the following four components together will constitute qualifier candidacy requirements for ph student and for ph candidate to be eligible for the enhanced srf fellowship completed course requirements with the minimum cgpa specified in section cleared comprehensive examination successful presentation on state of the art of the chosen field of research successful presentation and defense of research proposal the ph students are normally expected to complete successfully the qualifier requirements before the beginning of the fifth semester of his her registration in the ph program and in any case not later than the beginning of the sixth semester after their registration in the ph program part time candidates will need to complete the qualifier requirement before the beginning of the seventh semester comprehensive examination of ph tech ph student the comprehensive examination must be designed to test the general capability of the student and the breadth of his her knowledge in the discipline and areas related to the field of research the comprehensive examination shall be conducted by comprehensive examination committee of the department idrp the comprehensive examination will consist of written test with three papers departments will offer at least papers for conducting comprehensive examination each paper will have broad coverage of one essential sub area of the department the course content of these papers will be approved by the academic committee and the senate the syllabus of papers for the comprehensive examination will not be the same as courses offered by the department it must be designed to test the breadth of the knowledge in that area the src will specify set three papers as comprehensive requirement for particular student these three papers may be selected from across the departments the comprehensive examination requirements shall be intimated to the ph student within two weeks of src formation all comprehensive examinations will be scheduled on two fixed days in year it can coincide with the annual progress evaluation day of doctoral candidates students may decide to appear for three papers on the same day or on different days student can appear in the comprehensive examination before he she has completed the course requirements and satisfied the minimum specified cgpa requirement if the performance of the ph student in comprehensive examination paper in the first attempt is not satisfactory he she will be given one more opportunity to appear within six months of the first attempt for clearing of the comprehensive examination student must perform satisfactorily in all papers comprehensive examination to be completed by the students ph within semesters direct ph and mtech phd dual degree within semesters state of art seminar sota every ph student is required to give general seminar in the department covering the state of art of the area of research the presentation must also include patent landscaping of the area the presentation will be evaluated by the src candidate must have satisfactory grade in sota awarded by src for becoming eligible to present his research proposal research proposal research proposal report presentation will be evaluated by src after successful completion of sota the research proposal must include representative research work equivalent to research work worth credits src will allocate letter grade based on the performance of the candidate candidacy for the ph degree back to index student enrolled in the ph program is formally admitted to the candidacy for the ph degree after he she has completed the qualifier requirements for the degree only such students who are admitted to the candidacy will be allowed to submit ph thesis relaxation in tech ph dual degree program back to index tech ph dual degree students who have successfully completed all qualifier requirements under exceptional conditions as approved by src after years can also convert into part time external ph student and exit with tech degree if all conditions for part time external conversion are satisfied the renewal of their registration for every semester however will be considered only if src finds their progress to be satisfactory and recommends the continuance of registration cancellation of registration back to index the registration of student whose progress is not found to be satisfactory by the src or who has not enrolled will be liable for cancellation the registration of student who has not submitted his her thesis before the end of the maximum permissible period specified in section will be liable for cancellation synopsis back to index synopsis will consist of an open seminar and comprehensive internal closed door assessment of the research work through pre synopsis report by src the student can submit the synopsis only if the src is satisfied with the quality and quantity of the work for submission as ph thesis publications arising out of the thesis are to be submitted along with the pre synopsis report students should submit the synopsis and thesis within six months of the open seminar date if required an extension of three months may be permitted by dean academics on the recommendation of src if the synopsis and thesis are not submitted in the specified period the student will be asked to present the synopsis again on satisfactory completion of the prescribed courses with minimum cgpa specified in the comprehensive examination the sota the research work and the synopsis the student shall submit the requisite copies of the synopsis of his her research work in the required format through the supervisor and hod to the academic section for consideration of the src the student should have at least one paper either published or accepted for publication in refereed journal refereed conference src members are required to certify the quality of journals conference thesis submission and evaluation back to index the supervisor shall propose list of examiners consisting of at least four faculty members from abroad and faculty members from india who have the expertise in the area in which the student undertook research for selecting an examiner the following guidelines should be followed the examiners shall have at least years of post ph experience no two proposed examiners shall be from the same organization and the examiners can be faculty members or scientists of standing and repute chairman senate may ask for additional names for examiners the chairman senate shall select minimum two examiners from the proposed list of which at least one should be an examiner from outside india the consent of these examiners shall be taken before sending the thesis to them in addition src and supervisor shall be the examiners of the thesis the viva voce will be conducted in the presence of src supervisor and the external examiner one of the external examiners shall attend the thesis defense the examiners shall submit written report on the thesis within period of two months from the date of receipt of the thesis if both examiners declare the thesis as acceptable for award of ph degree the dean academics shall request the supervisor to hold the thesis defense by the student if any of the examiners reject the thesis for the award of the ph degree the dean academics shall report the matter to the chairman senate for further consideration the chairman senate will refer the thesis to third examiner under special circumstances else the registration of the student shall stand cancelled in the ph program if both examiners reject the thesis for the award of the ph degree no degree shall be awarded by the institute and the registration of the student shall stand cancelled in the ph program if an examiner suggests revision of the thesis the student shall resubmit the thesis after the revision within prescribed time period of months in consultation with the supervisor when both examiners recommend the thesis as accepted for the student to defend the thesis or after the resubmission of the thesis after incorporating the suggestions corrections given by the examiners the student shall publicly present the thesis and defend the contention of the thesis the committee consisting of chairman src supervisor the examiner from within india and other faculty members quorum would be chairman src supervisor and an external examiner who participated in the comprehensive examination of the student shall evaluate the thesis defense of the ph student also on their recommendation dean academics shall recommend to senate to consider the award of ph degree to the student graduation requirements back to index student is deemed to have completed the requirements for graduation if she he has met
