the process of admission for all the programs offered by the institute normally is underway
during april may for semester and during november december for semester in addition
the department may process applications for admissions to phd programs on continuous basis
and admit students as per the existing procedure
categories of admission
candidate can be admitted in any one of the following categories
full time regular
full time sponsored
however all categories are not applicable for all pg programs further programmes can be
offered in combination of these modes like fully sponsored part time program
full time regular
in campus student who can register for up to full credit permissible per semester student
supported by project of the institute will be considered full time regular student
ii full time sponsored
in campus student who can register for up to full credit permissible per semester the candidate
is sponsored either by his her employer or by self self sponsored candidate must have two
years of relevant industrial academic experience
iii part time
part time student is working professional who while employed attend regular classes as
per the schedule of the institute the student must be employed in the neighbourhood of iit
jodhpur the student must produce noc from the employer for pursuing the programme at
iit jodhpur the student can register only for limited number of credits as compared to
full time regular student
student working in an industry establishment academic institution which is equipped
with the necessary research and library facilities the employer must relieve the student to stay
in the campus to complete the minimum residency requirements
executive only for tech
professional who can carry out complete the programme requirement in
an accelerated fashion minimum in months or
accumulates credits as per convenience and petitions degree in maximum of years
the part time or full time mode by attending courses offered in synchronized remote
contact mode and limited direct interaction

maximum of days in an academic year including leave on medical grounds mid
semester break the student must apply for leave in advance even during the summer winter
term or mid semester break
phd student cannot avail leave for more than days at stretch
an tech sc student cannot avail leave for more than days at stretch
the leave beyond days in an academic year may be granted in exceptional cases by drc
without assistantship during that period
maternity leave for ph students is sanctioned as per the directives of mhrd it will not be
counted towards the maximum permissible duration of the programme
any other leave may also be permissible as per the guidelines of mhrd
may be applicable in unforeseen circumstances or for medical reasons absence for period of
four or more weeks in any semester will result in automatic withdrawal from that semester
in all such cases the fellowship will be stopped with immediate effect and it will be continued
for only after the student rejoins the institute drc can approve and intimate office of
academics regarding the leave of the student for records in case the leave extends beyond
semester it can only be approved through the academic committee semester withdrawal on
the medical ground will not be counted towards the maximum permissible duration of the
programme for the student

experimental work training using specialized facility not available at iitj
attending conferences workshops summer winter schools symposium
collaborative work as part of joint tech ph supervision
collaborative work for specific problem related to his ongoing ph programme
indicated in his research proposal
exchange program as part of an exchange program with sister institution in india or
all such requests must be evaluated and approved by src drc irc before the leave is granted

admitted in the department and no supervisor shall be
assigned at the time of selection

students and supervisor
for both ph and tech ph dual degree supervisor and area identification
must be completed by the end of the first semester
the convener drc department research committee coordinator interdisciplinary
research program would advise until the student is assigned to regular supervisor
there shall not be more than two supervisors in general for student additional
supervisor can be allowed with the approval of chairman senate
supervisor from outside the institute before the qualifier may be appointed on the
request of student supervisor with the recommendation of the drc irc and the dean
academics and approval of the chairman senate
the external supervisor will be requested to sign intellectual property right ipr and
non disclosure agreement nda documents as part of acceptance from the financial
point of view the institute will have no obligation to the external supervisor
caretaker supervisor additional supervisor
whenever the supervisor proceeds on short leave for period up to one year the
drc irc interdisciplinary research committee shall appoint caretaker supervisor in
consultation with the supervisor and the student to take care of the administrative
whenever the supervisor proceeds on long leave for period more than year then an
additional supervisor needs to be appointed on the suggestion of the supervisor
the supervisor going on lien or sabbatical may continue supervising students and the
supervisor can opt for either an additional supervisor or caretaker supervisor
the supervisor on his her retirement or on resignation may continue as supervisor and
will have to opt for an additional supervisor provided the student has cleared qualifier
before the supervisor retirement resignation
composition of departmental research committee drc
the drc will consist of coordinators of tech tech ph dual degree and ph programs
of the department head of the department and senior professor associate professor proposed
by the head the drc will be chaired by professor associate professor nominated by head of
the department the chairman of the drc will be member of the academic committee the
drc has to be approved by dean academics ph program coordinator will be the convenor
of drc and will be proposed by the head the tenure for the drc will be years
composition of interdisciplinary research committee irc
the irc will consist of all coordinators of idrps and senior professor associate professor as the
chairman of the irc will be nominated by dean academics the chairman of irc will be
member of ac one of the idrp co ordinators would be convenor of the committee the tenure
for the irc will be years the irc will be approved by the dean academics

qualifier requirements of ph student
the following four components together will constitute qualifier candidacy requirements for
ph student and for ph candidate to be eligible for the enhanced srf fellowship
completed course requirements with the minimum cgpa specified in section
cleared comprehensive examination
successful presentation on state of the art of the chosen field of research
successful presentation and defense of research proposal
the ph students are normally expected to complete successfully the qualifier requirements
before the beginning of the fifth semester of his her registration in the ph program and
in any case not later than the beginning of the sixth semester after their registration in
the ph program part time candidates will need to complete the qualifier requirement before
the beginning of the seventh semester
comprehensive examination of ph tech ph student
the comprehensive examination must be designed to test the general capability of the
student and the breadth of his her knowledge in the discipline and areas related to the
field of research
the comprehensive examination shall be conducted by comprehensive examination
committee of the department idrp
the comprehensive examination will consist of written test with three papers
departments will offer at least papers for conducting comprehensive examination
each paper will have broad coverage of one essential sub area of the department the
course content of these papers will be approved by the academic committee and the
senate the syllabus of papers for the comprehensive examination will not be the same
as courses offered by the department it must be designed to test the breadth of the
knowledge in that area
the src will specify set three papers as comprehensive requirement for particular
student these three papers may be selected from across the departments
the comprehensive examination requirements shall be intimated to the ph student
within two weeks of src formation
all comprehensive examinations will be scheduled on two fixed days in year it can
coincide with the annual progress evaluation day of doctoral candidates students may
decide to appear for three papers on the same day or on different days
student can appear in the comprehensive examination before he she has completed
the course requirements and satisfied the minimum specified cgpa requirement
if the performance of the ph student in comprehensive examination paper in the
first attempt is not satisfactory he she will be given one more opportunity to appear
within six months of the first attempt
for clearing of the comprehensive examination student must perform satisfactorily in
comprehensive examination to be completed by the students
ph within semesters
direct ph and mtech phd dual degree within semesters
state of art seminar sota
every ph student is required to give general seminar in the department covering the state
of art of the area of research the presentation must also include patent landscaping of the
area the presentation will be evaluated by the src candidate must have satisfactory
grade in sota awarded by src for becoming eligible to present his research proposal
research proposal report presentation will be evaluated by src after successful completion
of sota the research proposal must include representative research work equivalent to
research work worth credits src will allocate letter grade based on the performance of the
candidacy for the ph degree
student enrolled in the ph program is formally admitted to the candidacy for the ph
degree after he she has completed the qualifier requirements for the degree only such
students who are admitted to the candidacy will be allowed to submit ph thesis

cancellation of registration
the registration of student whose progress is not found to be satisfactory by the src
or who has not enrolled will be liable for cancellation
the registration of student who has not submitted his her thesis before the end of the
maximum permissible period specified in section will be liable for cancellation
synopsis will consist of an open seminar and comprehensive internal closed door
assessment of the research work through pre synopsis report by src
the student can submit the synopsis only if the src is satisfied with the quality and
quantity of the work for submission as ph thesis
publications arising out of the thesis are to be submitted along with the pre synopsis
students should submit the synopsis and thesis within six months of the open seminar
date if required an extension of three months may be permitted by dean academics
on the recommendation of src
if the synopsis and thesis are not submitted in the specified period the student will be
asked to present the synopsis again
on satisfactory completion of the prescribed courses with minimum cgpa specified in
the comprehensive examination the sota the research work and the synopsis
the student shall submit the requisite copies of the synopsis of his her research work in
the required format through the supervisor and hod to the academic section for
consideration of the src
the student should have at least one paper either published or accepted for publication
in refereed journal refereed conference src members are required to certify the
quality of journals conference
thesis submission and evaluation
the supervisor shall propose list of examiners consisting of at least four faculty
members from abroad and faculty members from india who have the expertise in the area in
which the student undertook research for selecting an examiner the following guidelines
should be followed
the examiners shall have at least years of post ph experience
no two proposed examiners shall be from the same organization and
the examiners can be faculty members or scientists of standing and repute
chairman senate may ask for additional names for examiners
the chairman senate shall select minimum two examiners from the proposed list of
which at least one should be an examiner from outside india the consent of these
examiners shall be taken before sending the thesis to them in addition src and
supervisor shall be the examiners of the thesis
the viva voce will be conducted in the presence of src supervisor and the
one of the external examiners shall attend the thesis defense
the examiners shall submit written report on the thesis within period of two months
from the date of receipt of the thesis
if both examiners declare the thesis as acceptable for award of ph degree the dean
academics shall request the supervisor to hold the thesis defense by the student
if any of the examiners reject the thesis for the award of the ph degree the dean
academics shall report the matter to the chairman senate for further consideration
circumstances else the registration of the student shall stand cancelled in the ph
if both examiners reject the thesis for the award of the ph degree no degree shall be
awarded by the institute and the registration of the student shall stand cancelled in the
if an examiner suggests revision of the thesis the student shall resubmit the thesis
after the revision within prescribed time period of months in consultation with the
when both examiners recommend the thesis as accepted for the student to defend the
suggestions corrections given by the examiners the student shall publicly present the
thesis and defend the contention of the thesis
the committee consisting of chairman src supervisor the examiner from within
india and other faculty members quorum would be chairman src supervisor and
an external examiner who participated in the comprehensive examination of the
recommendation dean academics shall recommend to senate to consider the award
of ph degree to the student

indian institute of technology jodhpur
academic programmes at indian institute of technology jodhpur are designed to develop the
highest calibre human resource capable of understanding the new patterns of knowledge
creation across disciplines obliterating traditional boundaries between science humanities
social sciences and engineering iit jodhpur aims to produce quality professionals who would be
able to address profound and wide ranging societal challenges of the st century such as
knowledge iit jodhpur endeavours to inculcate human qualities of courage integrity fairness
extra curricular activities on campus
the undergraduate academic programmes focus on developing temper for the life long
process of learning creative thinking and exploring the postgraduate academic programmes
focus on developing deep understanding of the subject of study coupled with creative
inquisitiveness and the ability to address and solve new problems with free and objective
the academic programmes are based on three tenets of semester system credit
system and relative grading these academic programmes are administered by duly
constituted academic committee ac through the office of academics
the ac will be chaired
by dean academics in the absence of dean academics associate dean academics
pg associate dean academics ug will discharge the responsibilities of dean academics
the senate of the institute has formulated set of guidelines and rules to ensure high
standard of performance as well as for smooth functioning of the academic programmes within
this broad set of guidelines subject to the approval of senate different programmes can
include additional academic requirements as deemed necessary for that programme these
modifications improvements as and when necessary
the academic session normally runs from the end of july in one year to the middle of july in the
next year the academic session is divided into three parts two regular semesters and
summer term as per the following timelines
semester from the fourth week of july to the last week of november
semester ii from the last week of december to the last week of april
summer term from the middle of may to the middle of july
excluding the days of the examinations the total number of days of instruction in semester is
the academic calendar gives the exact dates of all important events during the academic
session such as orientation registration the commencement of classes adding and dropping
of courses submission of documents examinations submission of grades project evaluation
declaration of results mid semester recess and vacation this calendar is approved by the
registration students are required to register for prescribed credits as per the programme
on the dates specified in the academic calendar if the student does not register by the date of
registration she he can register by paying the fine and register before the date of late
provisional registration fresh student joining the institute who is awaiting the final
results of the qualifying examination is allowed to register provisionally on submission of
certificate from her his last institute stating that she he has appeared in the final examination
of the qualifying degree the student is required to submit documents of having passed the
qualifying examination by the last date given in the academic calendar for the registration to be
late registration if the student does not register by the date of late registration as
deregistration may be made to chairman senate through dean academics chairman senate
may permit the continuation of registration on payment of an appropriate fine

approval of courses
the senate approves each course along with its weight in terms of credits only the approved
courses may be offered during any semester summer term
list of courses
the list of courses to be offered in program is finalized before the beginning of the semester
by the department hosting that program
categories of courses
courses offered can be from one of the following categories
regular course has hours of classroom engagement per one credit regular course can be
under elective or core compulsory categories
elective courses of or level will run if minimum of students
registers for the course or level elective course can run with minimum of
registered students course not running as regular course may be offered as self study
course as per the following section
self study course
self study course will be from the list of courses approved by senate the main features of
self study course are as follows
student may be allowed to register for an elective course as self study course
provided that the course is not running in that semester as regular course or student
is not on campus during the course with prior approval of the competent authority
student may also be permitted to register for core or program compulsory course in
self study mode provided he she has failed in it earlier and the course is not being
offered as regular course during that semester or student is not on campus during
the course with prior approval of the competent authority
students should apply for self study course with the appropriate recommendation of
course coordinator and dugc drc irc the final sanction of self study course to
student is made by the dean academics
formal classroom engagement may not be there for self study course but laboratory
design and computation exercises will be conducted if they form an integral part of the
the course coordinator conducts the assessment as per the evaluation norms for the
award of letter grade at the end of the semester
self study course will appear with the approved course title on the transcript
not exceeding of the total graded credit can be opted as self study course
independent study course
independent study enables student to pursue course credit on an academic topic of interest
under the supervision of faculty member the term independent does not mean not involving
an instructor but independent of regular class engagement self disciplined and having sense
of own direction and goals are fundamental requirements of an independent study course
student having cgpa more than or equal to can opt for independent study courses with the
recommendation of supervising professor the main features of an independent study course
are as follows
student may be permitted to register for topic of interest as an independent study
course not exceeding credits in self study mode at most once during the program
such independent study course will be counted toward open elective requirements of the
program and will appear with the title independent study on the transcript
recommendation of course coordinator and dugc drc irc the final sanction of an
independent study course to student is made by the dean academics
laboratory design and computation exercises will be conducted if they form an integral
part of the course
the course will be arranged planned and managed by supervising professor the
course coordinator conducts the assessment as per the evaluation norms for the award
of letter grade at the end of the semester
conduct of courses
each course is conducted by the instructor with the assistance of the required number of tutors
as needed the instructor is responsible for conducting the course evaluating the performance
of students awarding the grades at the end of the semester and transmitting the grades as per
the student shall have access to his her answer paper of all the written examinations
conducted for given course which may be shown to him her by the instructor concerned
the instructor must keep all evaluation records in his custody at least for the next six months
course approved by the senate of iit jodhpur can be conducted through either direct
contact ii synchronized remote contact iii guided study mode or combination of these in
direct contact mode coordinator or instructor will have face to face physical interaction with
the students synchronized remote contact mode would require the faculty and or the students
to be concurrently connected to the classroom interaction via electronic conferencing involving
both audio and video communication
however there has to be direct interaction between
faculty and students for limited hours typically of the stipulated contact hours in guided
study mode faculty would guide single or group of students to take up the study of an
approved course via self learning and discussion oriented contact sessions this mode can be
also adopted for enabling student to take up study of new course not yet approved by the
senate under the supervision of faculty all formal evaluation component applicable to
courses being run through any one of the above mentioned modes will be conducted under
direct physical supervision of faculty all laboratory component of course requiring the use
of the specialized facility will be conducted through direct contact
the instructors and tutors for all courses to be offered during the semester are allocated by the
head of the department hosting the program when faculty members of other departments are
also required to participate in teaching particular course the allocation shall be done in
consultation with the head of that department
auditing of courses
student may audit course in addition to the prescribed academic load requirement with the
permission of dean academics on the recommendations of instructor of the course being
audited and the faculty advisor under this arrangement the course will be listed in the grade
card of the student
student should have full attendance in each course unless the student takes leave of absence
reasons the student has to attend every lecture tutorial or lab session the
attendance records must be made available to the student after every lecture even if the
student attendance falls below the student will be allowed to appear for the exams
students not meeting the attendance criterion of will be required to score at least grade
to pass course these students would be awarded grade if their marks are lower than the
cut off for grade in course
the performance of students in course is evaluated continuously using their interaction in the
classroom and performances in examinations the laboratory work if any and term papers
the performance of students in course is evaluated through examinations and on continuous
basis the senate will decide from time to time on the system of tests and examinations in each
subject in each semester
minor minor and major examinations are mandatory components of the evaluation of
regular week long lecture course the minor examinations shall be of minutes
duration and the major examination of minutes fractal courses less than credits
must have at least one examination
the total weightage of examination component three examinations for week long
course shall be between to of the total weightage of evaluation measure
evaluation policy has to be known from the first day of the class
the continuous evaluation may include but not limited to interaction in the classroom
quizzes assignments tutorials laboratory work term papers and projects

grade point averages
semester grade point average
the semester grade point average sgpa is weighted average of the grades earned by
student in all the courses credited by her him and reflects her his academic performance in the
respective semester if the grade points associated with the letter grades earned by student
in courses registered during semester are and the corresponding credits
then the sgpa is given by the following formula
the sgpa is calculated on the basis of grades obtained in all courses except audit courses and
courses in which grade is awarded registered in particular semester
cumulative grade point average
the cumulative grade point average cgpa indicates the overall academic performance of
student in all the courses registered up to the latest completed semester the cgpa is
computed similarly as the sgpa considering all the courses in all semesters the cgpa is
calculated on the basis of all pass grades except audit courses and
courses in which grade is awarded obtained in all completed semesters
the sgpa and cgpa calculation are based on credits earned completed at iit jodhpur alone
grade card and transcript
grade card shall be issued to each student at the end of each semester and transcript at
the end of the programme iit jodhpur grade card and transcript will only indicate the courses
credits and grades completed at iit jodhpur and the total number of credits without grades
earned in other academic institutions in particular semester if applicable
waiver of requirements in special cases
the rules and regulations procedures and requirements stated in this manual other than those
related to admissions to the academic programmes may be waived in special circumstances by
the ac on the recommendation of the department with the approval of chairman senate all
such exceptions have to be reported to the senate
make up examinations
student who has missed minor or the major examination due to genuine reasons like
illness etc may be permitted to write make up examination for the missed components the
student should make an application to the dean academics through the course instructor
within ten days from the date of the examination missed explaining the reasons for their
absence applications received after this period need not be entertained the permission to take
make up examination will be given under exceptional circumstances such as admission to
hospital due to illness student needs to produce the necessary document subject to one of
the following categories
students residing in the hostels should produce medical certificate issued by the
medical officer of the institute that he she was admitted to the hospital during the
period of the missed quiz exam
students residing in the hostels and taking medical consultation with outside doctors are
required to obtain written permission from the medical officer of the institute hospital
before they proceed for such consultation
students residing in the hostels but taking medical consultation with outside doctors are
required to obtain an endorsement on the certificate of treatment by the medical officer
of the institute hospital
student staying outside the campus permanently temporarily must produce
medical certificate from the registered medical practitioner and the same should be duly
endorsed by the parent guardian
slot wise make up examination for major will be held during the makeup supplementary
week as per academic calendar of the subsequent semester for those who are permitted to take
the make up examination student who misses this make up examination will not normally be
resulting in the student missing make up examination the chairman of the senate in
consultation with the dean of academics may permit the student to appear for make up
day before the end of the first week of the next semester under no
circumstances prorating can be done for the missed examinations or attendance
regulations for undergraduate programmes
iit jodhpur currently offers bachelor of technology tech programs and capability linked
specializations or department area specialization student can also opt for
entrepreneurship or department area specialization in engineering innovation
admissions to the tech programmes are made once year in july through the all india level
joint entrance examination jee conducted by iits the procedures and other requirements for
admission are specified in the jee information brochure brought out every year
cultural exchange programmes
foreign nationals under the cultural exchange fellowship
program of the government of india administered by indian council of cultural relations
iccr new delhi persons interested in these programs are required to apply through the
indian high commission embassy in their respective countries
change enhancement of program
student already admitted to tech programme may switch to another department through
branch change student can enhance his her programme to minor interdisciplinary area
tech in minor interdisciplinary area major department area
specialization leading to tech in department area minor in entrepreneurship minor in
entrepreneurship leading to tech in entrepreneurship and department area specialization in
engineering innovation through industrial translation the rules governing these changes are
given in section branch change and section for all others
the reservation policy of government of india will be followed
student exchange program
student exchange program provides for one two semester visit by students between the two
academic institutions on reciprocal basis the visiting student must be full time student
enrolled in degree program in their home institution the exchange program is open to
full time undergraduate and graduate students of each home institution it will be executed as
per the pre approved arrangement including an mou between the institutions
selection of students under such program will be made by the dugc after assessing the
preparedness of students to meet the requirements of the planned coursework research at the
host institution and the relevance of the planned coursework research to the enrolled degree
program visiting student may carry out research or take courses for credit or otherwise or
may use other academic facilities as per pre approved arrangement including an mou
under exchange program student of iit jodhpur can register at another academic institution
in india or abroad with the expectation of credit transfer up to credits per semester in lieu of
the course work or research work through pre approved arrangement including an mou
student may apply to dugc for waiver of credits from her his program
requirements which he thinks are equivalent to the courses successfully completed at the
visited academic institution as an exchange student with the application the student must
grades obtained by her him at the visited academic
institution as an exchange student and other documents material that the concerned dugc may
means it deems fit the
equivalent credits requirements for which the student may be given waiver in her his
programme at iit jodhpur dugc will submit its recommendations to course equivalence
committee for its approval moreover
the credits grades indicated in the grade sheet obtained from the academic institution in
which the student has completed the courses should be used by the student as part of
his her transcripts
iit jodhpur transcripts will only indicate the courses credits and grades completed at iit
jodhpur and the total number of credits without grades earned in other academic
institutions in particular semester
the cgpa calculation based on credits earned completed at iit jodhpur alone is to be
considered for award of prizes
the credits earned at the visited academic institutions will be taken into account for the
calculation of minimum required credits for the award of the degree
visiting student is student who is registered for degree in recognized institute or
university in india or abroad and who is officially permitted by that institute or university to
complete part of his her academic requirements at iit jodhpur for that purpose the visiting
student may carry out research or take courses for credit or otherwise or may use other
person can be admitted as visiting student on duly sponsored application to the dean
visiting student may be admitted for maximum period of one year visiting
student will be required to pay all applicable fees depending upon the status program and
students so admitted also will be governed by all rules regulations and discipline applicable to
regular students of the institute
cancellation of admission
students admitted provisionally or otherwise to any program shall submit copies of their mark
sheets provisional certificates etc of the qualifying examination and other documents by the
last date specified for the purpose in the academic calendar the senate reserves the right to
cancel the admission of any student who fails to submit the prescribed documents by the
specified date or to meet other stipulated requirement also the senate reserves the right to
cancel the admission at any later time if it is found that the student had provided some false
information or suppressed relevant information while seeking admission
fulfillment of admission requirements
admission to any undergraduate program requires that the applicant be eligible go through the
laid down admission procedure and pay the prescribed fees the senate should formally
approve all admissions to the undergraduate programmes

assistantship for tech tech dual degree programmes
the students of dual degree programmes will be considered for award of institute research
teaching assistantship if they have earned credits by the end of the eighth semester only
those students who have either qualified gate or have cgpa more than will be eligible for
this assistantship the assistantship will be provided for maximum period of months
beginning from the summer semester following the eighth semester provided the student is
registered for tech major project in that semester student availing assistantship will be
required to provide hours of assistance per week besides his her normal academic work for
continuation of assistantship student will need to secure sgpa of
student receiving assistantship will be eligible for total of days leave during the
month period he she will not be entitled to mid semester breaks winter and summer
students can register for courses during summer up to maximum of eight credits on payment
of registration fee at prescribed rates the summer term is not regular semester and only
academically deficient students who have low cgpa and or fewer credits than advised by the
curriculum till that point in the programme major students minor students and such students
who are short of maximum eight credits to complete all graduation requirements may register
during this period
for core courses only students with failed backlog may be considered for summer registration
in case any vacancies are left in the courses being offered during the summer term once the
requirements of the above categories of students are fulfilled other students may register for
these courses to fulfil some of their graduation requirements in advance
the total number of contact hours for the courses remains the same as that during the regular
semesters and therefore the courses run at an accelerated pace the evaluation and grading
patterns also remain the same as during the regular semesters

termination from tech program
student may be terminated from the tech programme by ac if the student
is absent without authorized leave of absence for eight weeks or more in semester or
fails to report and register by the last date of registration without bonafide reason or
violates the code of conduct involves in ragging etc as confirmed by committee
constituted for the purpose or
does not earn the prescribed minimum number of credits within the maximum duration of
the program or
is on academic probation for two consecutive semesters
appeal against termination
student who is terminated from the tech program can appeal to the chairman senate for
reconsideration while making such an appeal the student is expected to give reasons for poor
academic performance and or why the termination should be reconsidered the senate shall
take final decision after considering all the available inputs but the senate will not entertain
any further appeal for review unless substantial additional information is brought to its notice
application for leave of absence should be addressed to the convener dugc and submitted
with medical certificate if applicable usually leave must not be availed of without prior
approval of the dugc
mid semester recess and vacation
undergraduate students are entitled to avail of mid semester recess and vacation as specified in
the academic calendar
student may be granted leave of absence during the semester for maximum of days on
medical grounds and for days for any other valid reason
it may be applicable in unforeseen circumstances or for medical reasons absence for period
of four or more weeks in any semester will result in automatic withdrawal from that semester
dugc can approve and intimate office of academics regarding the leave of the student for
records in case the leave extends beyond semester it can only be approved through the
academic committee semester withdrawal on the medical ground will not be counted towards
the maximum permissible duration of the programme for the student
to help students broaden their horizons and gain course work experience she he may be
permitted to proceed to other academic institutes industry organization in india or
abroad academic leave can be requested for any of the following reasons such as
experimental work training using specialized facility not available at iitj
exchange program as part of an exchange program with an academic institution in
india or abroad
all such requests must be evaluated and approved by dugc before the leave is granted
student may be allowed to spend maximum duration of one summer term and two
semesters on academic leave
student during academic leave can earn maximum of credits per semester as certified by
the dugc and approved by the course equivalence committee

categories of admission
candidate can be admitted in any one of the following categories
full time regular
full time sponsored
however all categories are not applicable for all pg programs further programmes can be
offered in combination of these modes like fully sponsored part time program
full time regular
in campus student who can register for up to full credit permissible per semester student
supported by project of the institute will be considered full time regular student
ii full time sponsored
in campus student who can register for up to full credit permissible per semester the candidate
is sponsored either by his her employer or by self self sponsored candidate must have two
years of relevant industrial academic experience
iii part time
part time student is working professional who while employed attend regular classes as
per the schedule of the institute the student must be employed in the neighbourhood of iit
jodhpur the student must produce noc from the employer for pursuing the programme at
iit jodhpur the student can register only for limited number of credits as compared to
full time regular student
student working in an industry establishment academic institution which is equipped
with the necessary research and library facilities the employer must relieve the student to stay
in the campus to complete the minimum residency requirements
executive only for tech
professional who can carry out complete the programme requirement in
an accelerated fashion minimum in months or
accumulates credits as per convenience and petitions degree in maximum of years
the part time or full time mode by attending courses offered in synchronized remote
contact mode and limited direct interaction

any other leave may also be permissible as per the guidelines of mhrd
may be applicable in unforeseen circumstances or for medical reasons absence for period of
four or more weeks in any semester will result in automatic withdrawal from that semester
in all such cases the fellowship will be stopped with immediate effect and it will be continued
for only after the student rejoins the institute drc can approve and intimate office of
academics regarding the leave of the student for records in case the leave extends beyond
semester it can only be approved through the academic committee semester withdrawal on
the medical ground will not be counted towards the maximum permissible duration of the
programme for the student

indicated in his research proposal

point of view the institute will have no obligation to the external supervisor
caretaker supervisor additional supervisor
whenever the supervisor proceeds on short leave for period up to one year the
drc irc interdisciplinary research committee shall appoint caretaker supervisor in
consultation with the supervisor and the student to take care of the administrative
whenever the supervisor proceeds on long leave for period more than year then an
additional supervisor needs to be appointed on the suggestion of the supervisor
the supervisor going on lien or sabbatical may continue supervising students and the
supervisor can opt for either an additional supervisor or caretaker supervisor
the supervisor on his her retirement or on resignation may continue as supervisor and
will have to opt for an additional supervisor provided the student has cleared qualifier
before the supervisor retirement resignation
composition of departmental research committee drc
the drc will consist of coordinators of tech tech ph dual degree and ph programs
of the department head of the department and senior professor associate professor proposed
by the head the drc will be chaired by professor associate professor nominated by head of
the department the chairman of the drc will be member of the academic committee the
drc has to be approved by dean academics ph program coordinator will be the convenor
of drc and will be proposed by the head the tenure for the drc will be years

the irc will consist of all coordinators of idrps and senior professor associate professor as the
chairman of the irc will be nominated by dean academics the chairman of irc will be
member of ac one of the idrp co ordinators would be convenor of the committee the tenure
for the irc will be years the irc will be approved by the dean academics

qualifier requirements of ph student
the following four components together will constitute qualifier candidacy requirements for
ph student and for ph candidate to be eligible for the enhanced srf fellowship
completed course requirements with the minimum cgpa specified in section
cleared comprehensive examination
successful presentation on state of the art of the chosen field of research
successful presentation and defense of research proposal
the ph students are normally expected to complete successfully the qualifier requirements
before the beginning of the fifth semester of his her registration in the ph program and
in any case not later than the beginning of the sixth semester after their registration in
the ph program part time candidates will need to complete the qualifier requirement before
the beginning of the seventh semester
comprehensive examination of ph tech ph student
the comprehensive examination must be designed to test the general capability of the
student and the breadth of his her knowledge in the discipline and areas related to the
field of research
the comprehensive examination shall be conducted by comprehensive examination
committee of the department idrp
the comprehensive examination will consist of written test with three papers
departments will offer at least papers for conducting comprehensive examination
each paper will have broad coverage of one essential sub area of the department the
course content of these papers will be approved by the academic committee and the
senate the syllabus of papers for the comprehensive examination will not be the same
as courses offered by the department it must be designed to test the breadth of the
knowledge in that area
the src will specify set three papers as comprehensive requirement for particular
student these three papers may be selected from across the departments
the comprehensive examination requirements shall be intimated to the ph student
within two weeks of src formation
all comprehensive examinations will be scheduled on two fixed days in year it can
coincide with the annual progress evaluation day of doctoral candidates students may
decide to appear for three papers on the same day or on different days
student can appear in the comprehensive examination before he she has completed
the course requirements and satisfied the minimum specified cgpa requirement
if the performance of the ph student in comprehensive examination paper in the
first attempt is not satisfactory he she will be given one more opportunity to appear
within six months of the first attempt
for clearing of the comprehensive examination student must perform satisfactorily in
comprehensive examination to be completed by the students
ph within semesters
direct ph and mtech phd dual degree within semesters
state of art seminar sota
every ph student is required to give general seminar in the department covering the state
of art of the area of research the presentation must also include patent landscaping of the
area the presentation will be evaluated by the src candidate must have satisfactory
grade in sota awarded by src for becoming eligible to present his research proposal
research proposal report presentation will be evaluated by src after successful completion
of sota the research proposal must include representative research work equivalent to
research work worth credits src will allocate letter grade based on the performance of the
candidacy for the ph degree
student enrolled in the ph program is formally admitted to the candidacy for the ph
degree after he she has completed the qualifier requirements for the degree only such
students who are admitted to the candidacy will be allowed to submit ph thesis
relaxation in tech ph dual degree program
requirements under exceptional conditions as approved by src after years can also
part time external
conditions for part time external conversion are satisfied
the renewal of their registration for every semester however will be considered only if
cancellation of registration
the registration of student whose progress is not found to be satisfactory by the src
or who has not enrolled will be liable for cancellation
the registration of student who has not submitted his her thesis before the end of the
maximum permissible period specified in section will be liable for cancellation
synopsis will consist of an open seminar and comprehensive internal closed door
assessment of the research work through pre synopsis report by src
the student can submit the synopsis only if the src is satisfied with the quality and
quantity of the work for submission as ph thesis
publications arising out of the thesis are to be submitted along with the pre synopsis
students should submit the synopsis and thesis within six months of the open seminar
date if required an extension of three months may be permitted by dean academics
on the recommendation of src
if the synopsis and thesis are not submitted in the specified period the student will be
asked to present the synopsis again
on satisfactory completion of the prescribed courses with minimum cgpa specified in
the comprehensive examination the sota the research work and the synopsis
the student shall submit the requisite copies of the synopsis of his her research work in
the required format through the supervisor and hod to the academic section for
consideration of the src
the student should have at least one paper either published or accepted for publication
in refereed journal refereed conference src members are required to certify the
quality of journals conference
thesis submission and evaluation
the supervisor shall propose list of examiners consisting of at least four faculty
members from abroad and faculty members from india who have the expertise in the area in
which the student undertook research for selecting an examiner the following guidelines
should be followed
the examiners shall have at least years of post ph experience
no two proposed examiners shall be from the same organization and
the examiners can be faculty members or scientists of standing and repute
chairman senate may ask for additional names for examiners
the chairman senate shall select minimum two examiners from the proposed list of
which at least one should be an examiner from outside india the consent of these
examiners shall be taken before sending the thesis to them in addition src and
supervisor shall be the examiners of the thesis
the viva voce will be conducted in the presence of src supervisor and the
one of the external examiners shall attend the thesis defense
the examiners shall submit written report on the thesis within period of two months
from the date of receipt of the thesis
if both examiners declare the thesis as acceptable for award of ph degree the dean
academics shall request the supervisor to hold the thesis defense by the student
if any of the examiners reject the thesis for the award of the ph degree the dean
academics shall report the matter to the chairman senate for further consideration
circumstances else the registration of the student shall stand cancelled in the ph
if both examiners reject the thesis for the award of the ph degree no degree shall be
awarded by the institute and the registration of the student shall stand cancelled in the
if an examiner suggests revision of the thesis the student shall resubmit the thesis
after the revision within prescribed time period of months in consultation with the
when both examiners recommend the thesis as accepted for the student to defend the
suggestions corrections given by the examiners the student shall publicly present the
